<script>
    document.getElementById('AmplitudeExpScript').addEventListener('load', function () {
        if (typeof window.ClickstreamAnalytics === 'undefined' || typeof Experiment === 'undefined') return;

        async function sendExposureEvent(exposure) {
            const options = {
                method: 'POST',
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    api_key: "426c0179737716bff762c26fe82535fa",
                    events: [
                        {
                            event_type: '$exposure',
                            device_id: localStorage.getItem('aws-solution/clickstream-web/deviceIdKey'),
                            user_id:
                                JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('aws-solution/clickstream-web/userAttributesKey'))?._user_id
                                    ?.value || null,
                            event_properties: {
                                flag_key: exposure.flag_key,
                                variant: exposure.variant,
                            },
                        },
                    ],
                }),
            };

            try {
                await fetch("https://api.eu.amplitude.com/batch", options);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error sending exposure');
            }
        }

        window.experiment = Experiment.Experiment.initialize(
            "client-KAon6nLqNqF70rQi4Cq4BVU6GBCJY4e8",
            {
                debug: "0" === '1',
                serverZone: 'eu',
                serverUrl: 'https://api.lab.eu.amplitude.com',
                exposureTrackingProvider: {
                    track: sendExposureEvent,
                },
            }
        );
    });
</script>

    <script>
        function getCookie(name) {
            var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]+)'));
            if (match) return match[2];
        }

        const getAnalyticsSearchId = () => {
            let id = getCookie('analyticsSearchId');
            const existingSearchParams = getCookie('analyticsSearchIdParams');
            const currentSearchParams = ['facilitator', 'London'].join('|');
            if (!id || existingSearchParams != currentSearchParams) {
                id = (Date.now() + Math.random()).toString(36);
                const now = new Date();
                now.setDate(now.getDate() + 7);
                const expiry = now.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = `analyticsSearchId=${id};expires=${expiry};path=/`;
                document.cookie = `analyticsSearchIdParams=${currentSearchParams};expires=${expiry};path=/`;
            }
            return id;
        };
        const analyticsSearchId = getAnalyticsSearchId();
    </script>
    <script type="text/javascript">
        const dlTrackJobInteraction = (job) => {
            if (!job?.dataset?.jobId) return;

            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            dataLayer.push({
                JOB_ID: job.dataset.jobId,
                JOB_COMPANY_ID: job.dataset.companyId || "",
                JOB_COMPANY_NAME: job.dataset.companyName || "",
                JOB_TOWN: job.dataset.jobLocation || "",
                JOB_INDUSTRY: job.dataset.jobIndustry || "",
                JOB_SALARY: job.dataset.jobSalary || "",
                JOB_TITLE: job.dataset.jobTitle || "",
                JOB_TYPE: job.dataset.jobType || "",
                JOB_POSTED_DATE: job.dataset.jobPosted || "",
                
            });
        };

        document.addEventListener("click", (e) => {
            if (e.target.closest("[datalayer-track-click]")) {
                const job = e.target.closest("article.job");
                dlTrackJobInteraction(job);
            }
        });

                var criteria = {"salary_type":null,"salary_min":"","location":"/locations/euro_regions/London","salary_band_ids":null,"distance":15,"type":[],"salary_max":"","salary_band_annual":[],"keywords":"facilitator","category_prefix":null,"industry":null,"salary_period":"annum","geo":"London"};

                firebase.messaging().getToken()
                .then( function(token) {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        url: "/search-jobs-push-alerts/register",
                        contentType: 'application/json',
                        data: JSON.stringify({ token: token, criteria: criteria }),
                    });
                })
                .catch(function() { });
            }

            $(function() {
                // Browser doesn't support the APIs required to use the firebase SDK
                if (!firebase.messaging.isSupported()) return;

                firebase.initializeApp({"storageBucket":"cv-library.appspot.com","authDomain":"cv-library.firebaseapp.com","messagingSenderId":"618559594986","apiKey":"AIzaSyBqdocaT9EMcqJX4xQ-jpZzQIamDFvF9hI","measurementId":"G-VT9FHLL2J9","projectId":"cv-library","appId":"1:618559594986:web:0e999bba7dbcc23b475293","databaseURL":"https://cv-library.firebaseio.com"});

                firebase.messaging().onMessage(function(payload) {
                    // Intercept payload on page
                })

                if (!("Notification" in window)) {
                    // Browser does not support desktop notification
                    return;
                }

                else if (Notification.permission === "granted") {
                    save_search_criteria();
                }

                
                else if (Notification.permission !== "denied") {
                    Notification.requestPermission()
                    .then(function (permission) {
                        if (permission === "granted") save_search_criteria();
                    })
                    .catch(function() { });
                }
            });
        });
    </script>
